The architecture-specific x86_64 implementation is in gcc/config/i386/i386.cc, which contains three key functions: ix86_expand_prologue (line 9133) which expands the prologue and handles stack probing during function setup, get_probe_interval (line 6936) which determines the probing interval based on the protection settings, and ix86_target_stack_probe (line 996) which checks if target-specific stack probing should be used. The generic stack clash expansion logic is implemented in gcc/explow.cc, which defines two critical functions: anti_adjust_stack_and_probe_stack_clash (line 2072) for stack clash-specific probing that probes every allocated page, and anti_adjust_stack_and_probe (line 2201) for standard stack adjustment with probing. Function declarations are exported in gcc/explow.h. The target hook infrastructure for stack clash protection is defined through TARGET_STACK_CLASH_PROTECTION_ALLOCA_PROBE_RANGE, which has a default implementation in gcc/targhooks.cc (line 2747, function default_stack_clash_protection_alloca_probe_range) and is declared in gcc/targhooks.h (line 305). Architecture-specific implementations override this hook in aarch64.cc (line 33925) and riscv.cc (line 16848). Validation of the stack clash protection implementation is performed through test cases in gcc/testsuite/gcc.target/i386/stack-clash-protection.c, which verifies that the -fstack-clash-protection flag properly instruments code to defend against stack clash attacks.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
